With striking round rollers, a sleek wheel featuring precision knurling on the outer rim, and knurling detailing on the handle, this tub door exudes a refined modern touch. Engineered for precision and ease, the Elan Cass features RollerDisk™ for up to 3/8 in. adjustment and SmartAdjust™ for an additional 1/2 in. adaptability, ensuring a perfect fit. For silent and smooth operation, LockTrack™, aerodynamic rollers, and a built-in door stopper work together to provide effortless glide and stability. VIGO enhances your shower with high performance, seamless functionality, and a spacious, modern feel.

- [Arden Frameless Fixed Shower Screen](https://vigoindustries.com/products/vg6094): Introducing the VIGO Arden Frameless Fixed Shower Screen, a modern and durable addition to any bathroom. Measuring 34 in. in width and 78 in. in height, this sleek screen features fluted tempered glass and a stainless steel finish, ensuring resistance to scratches, corrosion, and daily wear for a lasting polished appearance. For enhanced stability, the Arden uses two solid brass brackets for secure wall mounting and reliable anchoring. Equipped with Seal-Thru™, full-length vertical and bottom seals prevent leaks, keeping your bathroom clean and dry. The European-style arched glass panel creates a minimalist aesthetic, seamlessly blending with contemporary interiors. VIGO elevates your shower experience with a frameless design that enhances openness, delivers lasting performance, and adds a touch of refined style.

- [Arden Framed Fixed Shower Screen](https://vigoindustries.com/products/vg6078): The Arden Framed Fixed Shower Screen by VIGO is designed to bring modern elegance and durability to any bathroom. Measuring 34 in. wide and 78 in. high, it offers a sleek, contemporary look while ensuring long-lasting performance. Crafted with clear tempered glass and a stainless steel finish, this sleek screen is scratch-resistant, corrosion-proof, and built to withstand daily wear, ensuring a refined look that lasts. For enhanced stability, the Arden features vertical and bottom rail support, providing secure wall anchoring for long-term durability. Seal-Thru™ incorporates full-length vertical and bottom seals to create a watertight barrier, preventing leaks and keeping your bathroom clean and dry. With its European-style arched glass panel, this shower screen embodies sleek minimalism, seamlessly blending with contemporary interiors. VIGO enhances your shower with a framed design that balances structural support with a modern, open feel - perfect for contemporary spaces.
